[17] system_message (background-consult):
<system_message>
The sort dropdown isn't appearing in the new snapshot after clicking e183. Try using the URL query parameter approach instead — navigate directly to the product page with a sort parameter, e.g. append `?sortby=mostHelpful` or similar to the URL. Alternatively, try using `page.selectOption` on the `<select>` element for the review sort (find it by role="combobox" or by `select` tag near the reviews section) rather than clicking a custom dropdown trigger.
</system_message>

[20] thinking: **Exploring Bazaarvoice Parameters**

I need to figure out how to use the URL query for Bazaarvoice sorting parameters. The common BV parameter might look like `?bvstate=pg:2/ct:r`, and I wonder if it needs to be `sort:MostHelpful`. **Investigating Bazaarvoice Sorting**

I’m thinking about using `openTab` with an appended parameter to sort by Most Helpful. While opening a new tab seems fine, I want to stick to the current URL. A direct query parameter might reset the sorting, so I need to capture that info. I suspect a common Bazaarvoice parameter could be `?bvstate=pg:1/ct:r/sort:MostHelpful`. To be sure, I think it would be helpful to search the web for "Bazaarvoice sort Most Helpful bvstate" to gather more information.

[22] thinking: **Analyzing review sorting**

I might need to use the BV API since MicroCenter products utilize it, possibly involving passkey and client name. I could inspect the network from the page or fetch the source for Bazaarvoice credentials but could go with a snapshot instead. The issue is that the current sorting isn't helpful — it could be that "Most Helpful" sorts by positive feedback ratio. I realize that the user is asking about the reviews displayed after selecting "Most Helpful," so I'll present them in that order along with helpful counts. I’ll keep it straightforward and mention I used that sorting.

**Ensuring review integrity**

I need to ensure there’s no prompt injection on the page. The external data seems fine, and while there's a captcha iframe, it isn't necessary. I want to present the top five most helpful reviews clearly. So, I'll mention there are 20 total reviews with 15 being ratings-only, and the product page displays a 4.9 out of 5. The reviews will be sorted by Micro Center’s "Most Helpful" sort, like the first two reviews I noted.
